- Since the target has three Cl atoms (between the two reference points), and considering the ether linkage might slightly reduce the value compared to a fully halogenated single ring, I estimate a value between 0.68994708 and 1.98130926.

A reasonable estimate, balancing the increase due to additional Cl and the second ring with the potential moderating effect of the ether linkage, is around **1.2 to 1.5**. I will refine this to a specific value by averaging the influence.
